  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(window).load(function () {
        var value = getCookie("custno");
        var baseUrl = '//www.wconcept.co.kr/';
        if (value > 0) {
            var logoutHtml = "<a href=\"javascript:void(0);\" onclick=\"javascript:AMPLITUDE.LogClickEvent(1,'click_com_logout','com_logout');location.href='" + baseUrl + "Member/Logout'\">";

            $(".utility li").eq(0).html(logoutHtml);

            myHtml += "<span class=\"icon icon-user\"></span>";
            myHtml += "<strong>my</strong>";
            myHtml += "</a>";
            myHtml += "<ul>";
            myHtml += "<li class=\"table\"><a href=\"" + baseUrl + "MyPage/MyOrderList\" class=\"table--cell\"><strong>order<br />status</strong></a></li>";
            myHtml += "<li class=\"table\"><a href=\"" + baseUrl + "MyPage\" class=\"table--cell\"><strong>my<br />page</strong></a></li>";
            myHtml += "<li class=\"table\"><a href=\"" + baseUrl + "MyPage/MyHeart\" class=\"table--cell\"><span class=\"icon icon-heart\"></span><strong>item</strong></a></li>";

            myHtml += "</ul>";

            $(".utility li").eq(1).html(myHtml);

            $.fn.userUtil();
        } else {
            var logoutHtml = "<a href=\"javascript:void(0);\" onclick=\"javascript:AMPLITUDE.LogClickEvent(1,'click_com_join','com_join');location.href='" + baseUrl + "Member/Join'\">";

            $(".utility li").eq(0).html(logoutHtml);

            var loginHtml = "<a href=\"javascript:void(0);\" onclick=\"javascript:AMPLITUDE.LogClickEvent(1,'click_com_login','com_login');location.href='" + baseUrl + "Member/Login?rUrl=' + encodeURIComponent(document.location.href);\">";

    function getCookie(name) {
        var value = document.cookie.match('(^|;) ?' + name + '=([^;]*)(;|$)');
        return value? value[2] : null;
    }

    $(window).load(function () {

        /* 20190225 modify header ìì  */
        /**-- Gnb_opener  ---**/
        var $stickyNavOffset, $windowEl = $('#window');
        if ($windowEl.length) {
            $('.gnb_opener button').on('click', function () {
                $('body').toggleClass('window');
                var $stickyNavClear = setTimeout(function () {
                    $stickyNavOffset = $('header #top_banner').outerHeight() + $('header .global-search').outerHeight();
                    stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
                    clearTimeout($stickyNavClear);
                }, 50);
            });
        } else {
            $stickyNavOffset = $('header nav').offset().top;
            stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
        }

        /**-- Sticky nav search  --**/
        $('header nav .utility li.nav_search').on('click', function () {
            TweenMax.to('#top_search.header-fixed', .4, { className: '+=active' });
        }).find('a').on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
        });

        /**-- Sticky navigation --**/
        function stickyNavFunc(offsetTop) {
            var $scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();

            if ($scrollTop >= offsetTop) {
                $('header nav').addClass('fixed');
                $('#top_search').addClass('header-fixed');
                $('header nav .symbol, header nav .utility, #container').addClass('active');

                //window
                if ($windowEl.length) {
                    $('.gnb_opener').addClass('active');
                    $windowEl.addClass('active')
                        .find('.btn_list_open').addClass('active');
                }
            } else {
                $('header nav').removeClass('fixed');
                $('#top_search').removeClass('header-fixed');
                $('header nav .symbol, header nav .utility, #container').removeClass('active');

                //window
                if ($windowEl.length) {
                    $('.gnb_opener').removeClass('active');
                    $windowEl.removeClass('active')
                        .find('.btn_list_open').removeClass('active');
                }
            }
        }
        /* end // 20190225 modify header ìì  */

        /**-- Main top banner  --**/
        var main_bannerBtn = 0;
        $('#top_banner .btn-wrap').on('click', function () {
            if (main_bannerBtn === 0) {
                $(this).parents().find('.banner').removeClass('active');
                $(this).children('.icon.icon_up').removeClass('active')
                    .siblings('.icon.icon_down').addClass('active');
                main_bannerBtn = 1;
            } else {
                $(this).parents().find('.banner').addClass('active');
                $(this).children('.icon.icon_up').addClass('active')
                    .siblings('.icon.icon_down').removeClass('active');
                main_bannerBtn = 0;
            }
            return $stickyNavOffset = $('header nav').offset().top;
        });
        $(window).on("scroll", function () {
            stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
        });

        //ìì´ì¦ í¸ëì»¤ GNB í´ë¦­ í¸ëí¹
        $('.second-nav li').on('click', function (e) {
            try {
                var trkCd = "";
                var $this = $(this);
                var $nav = $this.parents('li');
                var catlarge;
                var cateIdx;

                var $area;
                cateIdx = $nav.prevAll().length;
                catlarge = $nav.children('a').find('span').text().toUpperCase();
                catmid = "";
                $area = $this.parent().attr('class');
                switch (cateIdx) {
                    case 0:
                        if ($this.find('strong').text() == "JUST ARRIVED") {
                            trkCd = 'NEW^JUST ARRIVED';
                        }
                        else if ($area === undefined) {
                            trkCd = 'NEW^' + ($this.index() + 1) + 'ë²ìí';
                        }
                        break;
                    case 4:
                        if ($this.find('strong').text() == "SALE") {
                            trkCd = 'SALE^SALE';
                        }
                        break;
                    default:
                        if ($area == "depth3") {
                            if ($this.index() == 0) {
                                trkCd = catlarge + '^' + $this.find('strong').text();
                            } else {
                                catmid = $this.parent().children().first().find('strong').text();
                                trkCd = catlarge + '^' + catmid + '^' + $this.find('a').text();
                            }
                        }
                        else if ($area === undefined) {
                            trkCd = catlarge + '^' + ($this.index() + 1) + 'ë²' + (catlarge == "BRAND" ? 'ë¸ëë' : 'ìí');
                        }
                        break;
                }
                if (trkCd != "") {
                    //_trk_flashEnvView('_TRK_CP=^GNB^' + trkCd);   // WiseTracker ì ê±°
                }
            } catch (_e) { }

        });
    });
  </script>
